<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-80" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-80"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Build-your-own, General purpose, Data analysis</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-79" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-79"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Superagent is not a single agent, but a tool that allows creating agents without coding</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Simplifies the configuration and deployment of LLM Agents to production</li>
<li>"One of the core principals of SuperAgent is to build with any third-party dependencies to proprietary tech"</li>
<li>It provides a range of features and functionalities to make it easier for developers to build, manage and deploy AI agents to production including features such as built in memory and document retrieval via vector dbs, powerful tools, webhooks, cron jobs etc.</li>
<li>There are two main types of agents: action agents and plan-and-execute agents</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-77" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-77"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-80" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-80"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">SuperAGI is an open-source autonomous AI framework to enable development and deployment autonomous agents</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>An AI agent framework</li>
<li>Open source, but infrastructure is -source</li>
<li>Features
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Provision, Spawn &amp; Deploy Autonomous AI Agents</li>
<li>Extend Agent Capabilities with Tools</li>
<li>Run Concurrent Agents Seamlessly</li>
<li>Graphical User Interface</li>
<li>Action Console</li>
<li>Multiple Vector DBs</li>
<li>Multi-Modal Agents</li>
<li>Agent Trajectory Fine-Tuning</li>
<li>Performance Telemetry</li>
<li>Optimized Token Usage</li>
<li>Agent Memory Storage</li>
<li>Looping Detection Heuristics</li>
<li>Concurrent Agents</li>
<li>Resource Manager</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">ä¿®å¤é—®é¢˜å’Œç¼–å†™ä»£ç çš„ Github åŠ©æ‰‹</font></font></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-82" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-82"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Sweep is a Github assistant the helps fix small bugs and implement small features</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>To install, click the install button</li>
<li>Then add the repository you want, make a quick ticket (e.g. writing tests)</li>
<li>Prepend the ticket with "Sweep:" and let Sweep handle the rest</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/seanpixel/Teenage-AGI/blob/main/README.md#experiments"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">é’å°‘å¹´AGI</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-teenage-agi" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šé’å°‘å¹´ AGI" href="#teenage-agi"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">BabyAGIçµæ„Ÿä»£ç†ï¼Œå¯å”¤èµ·æ— é™è®°å¿†</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/18cfdc02648d5adceb0e43e3ebb80742421d56122e2a76a1cc3f7ab7eafd6780/68747470733a2f2f6769746875622e6769746875626173736574732e636f6d2f6173736574732f4769744875622d4d61726b2d6561323937316365653739392e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/18cfdc02648d5adceb0e43e3ebb80742421d56122e2a76a1cc3f7ab7eafd6780/68747470733a2f2f6769746875622e6769746875626173736574732e636f6d2f6173736574732f4769744875622d4d61726b2d6561323937316365653739392e706e67" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://github.githubassets.com/assets/GitHub-Mark-ea2971cee799.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-85" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-85"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-84" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-84"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A BabyAGI-inspired agent that can recall infinite memory, "thinks" before making action, and doesn't lose memory after being shutting down</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Model: GPT-4</li>
<li>Language: Python</li>
<li>Uses OpenAI and Pinecone to give memory to an AI agent and also allows it to "think" before making an action (outputting text)</li>
<li>Also, just by shutting down the AI, it doesn't forget its memories since it lives on Pinecone and its memory counter saves the index that it's on</li>
<li>A process that happens every time the AI is queried by the user:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>AI vectorizes the query and stores it in a Pinecone Vector Database</li>
<li>AI looks inside its memory and finds memories and past queries that are relevant to the current query</li>
<li>AI thinks about what action to take</li>
<li>AI stores the thought from Step 3</li>
<li>Based on the thought from Step 3 and relevant memories from Step 2, AI generates an output</li>
<li>AI stores the current query and its answer in its Pinecone vector database memory</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-82" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-82"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Created by <a href="https://twitter.com/sean_pixel" rel="nofollow">@sean_pixel</a></li>
<li>Inspired by paper <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2304.03442" rel="nofollow">"Generative Agents: Interactive Simulacra of Human Behavior"</a></li>
</ul>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://vanna.ai/" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å‡¡çº³äººå·¥æ™ºèƒ½</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-vannaai" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šVanna.AI" href="#vannaai"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">åŸºäº Python çš„ AI SQL ä»£ç†æ ¹æ®æ‚¨çš„æ¶æ„è¿›è¡Œè®­ç»ƒ</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/29ecb34150d5e52a1d3dadf5bdb1f6abd0b9482f508700e7b6926e1d2827bb8b/68747470733a2f2f76616e6e612e61692f696d672f76616e6e612e737667"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/29ecb34150d5e52a1d3dadf5bdb1f6abd0b9482f508700e7b6926e1d2827bb8b/68747470733a2f2f76616e6e612e61692f696d672f76616e6e612e737667" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://vanna.ai/img/vanna.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-86" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-86"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Coding, Debugging, Code migration, Data analysis</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-85" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-85"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Vanna is an Open-Source Python-based AI SQL agent trained on your schema that writes complex SQL in seconds</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>AI-driven business intelligence assistant</li>
<li>Vanna helps you generate and run accurate SQL for your database using LLMs via Retrieval-Augmented Generation</li>
<li>Vanna works in two easy steps - train a RAG "model" on your data, and then ask questions which will return SQL queries that can be set up to automatically run on your database</li>
<li>The Vanna Python package and the various frontend integrations are all open-source</li>
<li>Vannaâ€™s capabilities are tied to the training data you give it. More training data means better accuracy for large and complex datasets</li>
<li>Your database contents are never sent to the LLM. The metadata storage layer only sees schemas, documentation, and queries</li>
<li>As you use Vanna more, your model continuously improves as we augment your training data</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-83" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-83"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://voyager.minedojo.org/" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">èˆªè¡Œè€…å·</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-voyager" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šèˆªæµ·è€…å·" href="#voyager"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">Minecraft ä¸­ç”± LLM æä¾›æ”¯æŒçš„ç»ˆèº«å­¦ä¹ ä»£ç†</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3e54567e4cd63cb2e8f7278913e2bcce22acf288248a36054277c7b521505f26/68747470733a2f2f766f79616765722e6d696e65646f6a6f2e6f72672f6173736574732f696d616765732f6578706c6f726174696f6e5f706572666f726d616e63652e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3e54567e4cd63cb2e8f7278913e2bcce22acf288248a36054277c7b521505f26/68747470733a2f2f766f79616765722e6d696e65646f6a6f2e6f72672f6173736574732f696d616765732f6578706c6f726174696f6e5f706572666f726d616e63652e706e67" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://voyager.minedojo.org/assets/images/exploration_performance.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-87" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-87"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-86" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-86"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A LLM-powered embodied lifelong learning agent in Minecraft that continuously explores the world, acquires diverse skills, and makes novel discoveries without human intervention</li>
<li>Voyager consists of three key components:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>an automatic curriculum that maximizes exploration</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li>an ever-growing skill library of executable code for storing and retrieving complex behaviors</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li>a new iterative prompting mechanism that incorporates environment feedback, execution errors, and self-verification for program improvement</li>
</ol>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Voyager interacts with GPT-4 via blackbox queries, which bypasses the need for model parameter fine-tuning</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-84" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-84"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-87" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-87"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å¤šæ™ºèƒ½ä½“ç¯å¢ƒæ¨¡æ‹Ÿåº“</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3a4f071169ca25d79edada31cda80a3b8f42dacf4b2db6fbf32a86d62b3050e8/68747470733a2f2f7468656f6c76732e6769746875622e696f2f77657374776f726c642f696d672f636f7665725f68715f77657374776f726c64312e6a7067"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3a4f071169ca25d79edada31cda80a3b8f42dacf4b2db6fbf32a86d62b3050e8/68747470733a2f2f7468656f6c76732e6769746875622e696f2f77657374776f726c642f696d672f636f7665725f68715f77657374776f726c64312e6a7067" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://theolvs.github.io/westworld/img/cover_hq_westworld1.jpg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-89" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-89"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-88" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-88"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A-  multi-agent simulation library, with a goal to simulate and optimize systems and environments with multiple agents interacting</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Researchers from Stanford and Google created an interactive sandbox env with 25 Gen AI agents can simulate human behavior</li>
<li>They walk in the park, join for coffee at a cafe, and share news with colleagues. They demonstrated surprisingly good social</li>
<li>Westworld's inspiration is drawn from Unity software and Unity ML Agents, adapted in Python</li>
<li>Languages
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The library is available on PyPi via pip install westworld</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/TheoLvs/westworldjs">Javascript version (being developed)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Features
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Easy creation of Grid and non-grid environments</li>
<li>Objects (Agents, Obstacles, Collectibles, Triggers)</li>
<li>Subclassing of different objects to create custom objects</li>
<li>Spawner to generate objects randomly in the environment</li>
<li>Basic rigid body system for all objects</li>
<li>Simple agent behaviors (pathfinding, wandering, random walk, fleeing, vision range)</li>
<li>Automatic maze generation</li>
<li>Layer integration to convert image to obstacle and snap it to a grid</li>
<li>Sample simulations and sample agents for classic simulations</li>
<li>Simulation visualization, replay and export (gif or video)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-86" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-86"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/TheoLvs/westworld">GitHub</a></li>
<li><a href="https://theolvs.github.io/westworld/" rel="nofollow">Documentation</a></li>
<li><a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2304.03442" rel="nofollow">Underlying paper - Generative Agents</a></li>
<li>A paper simulating interactions between tens of agents</li>
<li>Presenting an architecture that extends a language model to store and synthesize the agent's experiences, enabling dynamic behavior planning in an interactive sandbox environment with generative agents</li>
</ul>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/team-openpm/workgpt"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å·¥ä½œGPT</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-workgpt" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šWorkGPT" href="#workgpt"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">ç”¨äºè°ƒç”¨APIçš„GPTä»£ç†æ¡†æ¶</font></font></p>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/33294ae5cfb9159fe3deb6464d0580c0d1703b06e195d8e8b596ed9d32d6eb46/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f636172645f696d672f313734343930323331303333363131383738342f41566e44334d432d3f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/33294ae5cfb9159fe3deb6464d0580c0d1703b06e195d8e8b596ed9d32d6eb46/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f636172645f696d672f313734343930323331303333363131383738342f41566e44334d432d3f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://pbs.twimg.com/card_img/1744902310336118784/AVnD3MC-?format=jpg&amp;name=medium" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-90" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-90"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-89" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-89"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>WorkGPT is an agent framework in a similar fashion to AutoGPT or LangChain. You give it a directive and an array of APIs and it will converse back and forth with the AI until its directive is complete.</li>
<li>For example, a directive could be to research the web for something, to crawl a website, or to order you an Uber. We support any and all APIs that can be represented with an OpenAPI file.</li>
<li>WorkGPT now has OpenAI's new function invocation feature baked into it
<ul dir="auto">
<li>While chaining together APIs was possible before (see AutoGPT), it was slow, expensive, and error prone</li>
<li><a href="https://twitter.com/maccaw/status/1669367224694607875" rel="nofollow">The tweet announcing this feature</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">è§£å†³å„ç§ä»»åŠ¡çš„å®éªŒæ€§ LLM ä»£ç†</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/7aa38207de0d7a1f628fd2bf34838607ed633f16f7f04f0e8d4f8fafa78bc2c7/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f70726f66696c655f62616e6e6572732f313731333838313933343939313039333736302f313639373435363738322f3135303078353030"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/7aa38207de0d7a1f628fd2bf34838607ed633f16f7f04f0e8d4f8fafa78bc2c7/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f70726f66696c655f62616e6e6572732f313731333838313933343939313039333736302f313639373435363738322f3135303078353030" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_banners/1713881934991093760/1697456782/1500x500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-91" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-91"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose, Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-90" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-90"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">XAgent is an open-source experimental Large Language Model (LLM) driven autonomous agent that can automatically solve various tasks</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Emergence &amp; Autonomy</strong>: XAgent's autonomous operations transcend biases.</li>
<li><strong>Safety &amp; Operation</strong>: Secure execution within docker environments.</li>
<li><strong>Expert-Knowledge Free</strong>: Effective operation without sole expert reliance.</li>
<li><strong>Interface &amp; Interaction</strong>: Interact via a user-friendly GUI or command line, while it adapts and collaborates.</li>
<li><strong>Dual-loop Mechanism</strong>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Outer-Loop</strong>: Manages plans and task refinements.</li>
<li><strong>Inner-Loop</strong>: Dispatch, ReACT-based execution, feedback.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Universal Language - Function Calling</strong>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>ToolAgent &amp; ReACT</strong>: Optimal action series for subtasks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Tools</strong>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ğŸ“ File Editor</li>
<li>ğŸ“˜ Python Notebook</li>
<li>ğŸŒ Web Browser</li>
<li>ğŸ–¥ï¸ Shell</li>
<li>ğŸ§© Rapid API</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yeagerai/yeagerai-agent"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">yä»£ç†</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-yagents" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šyAgents" href="#yagents"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å…·å¤‡è®¾è®¡ã€ç¼–ç å’Œè°ƒè¯•å·¥å…·çš„èƒ½åŠ›</font></font></p>
<details>

<p dir="auto">Coding, Build-your-own</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-91" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-91"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">yAgents is an Agent-Builder Agent made by Yeager.ai capable of designing, coding and debugging its own tools.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Designed to help build, prototype, and deploy AI-powered tools and agents easily and efficiently.</li>
<li>Built on the LangChain framework, allowing users of any technical background to create, improve, and deploy AI agents.</li>
<li>Equipped with an interactive command line interface for real-time feedback and ease of navigation.</li>
<li>Features session persistent memory to ensure data preservation across multiple sessions</li>
<li>Quick and easy installation via pip.</li>
<li>Contributions to expand and improve yAgents are highly encouraged.</li>
<li>Warnings
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Requires GPT-4 API access.</li>
<li>Not tested for Windows systems</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>YC company</li>
<li>"Creating the first human-like digital workers, called Artisans"</li>
<li>Artisans are advanced human-like digital workers trained to do specific roles, who integrate alongside human teams</li>
<li>They have unique faces, names, memories &amp; skills, and they continuously improve once they are employed, molding to each company's needs</li>
<li>The first Artisan, Ava, automates the entire outbound sales process and can be set up with a 10-minute conversation. Ava creates TCPs, prospects with her database of over 270,000,000 contacts, crafts &amp; sends highly bespoke email sequences, and books meetings into your calendar. And, you can manage all features &amp; settings by talking to Ava via Slack.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-105" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-105"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>broadn is a no-code platform that helps non-technical people build AI products in minutes. We're faster and more flexible than traditional no-code tools through an LLM powered conversational interface and an agent architecture that automates complex backend/workflow operations</li>

<li>Dosu keeps a watchful eye on open issues, resolving those that you might have missed and deprecating issues that no longer exist. Itâ€™ll even ask you if itâ€™s not sure.</li>

<p dir="auto">Duckie AI is a platform that lets engineers manage a team of AI software development companions (Ducklings) that get their dev work done</p>

Ducklings chat with users to define their goals, come up with engineering designs, and generate code</li>

<p dir="auto">Build-your-own, General purpose</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">With Fine-Tuner, you can build sophisticated, tailored AI agents at scale without any need for technical skills or coding. Just bring your data and ideas, and we'll provide the toolset you need to transform them into powerful AI solutions, capable of handling vast amounts of data and users. Take advantage of our scalable platform to meet your growing needs with ease and efficiency</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Connecting Your Chatbot to Your App</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">FineTuner.ai is a no-code AI platform that enables users to create and deploy custom AI agents and components without any coding.
With an intuitive UI/UX and rapid API deployment, FineTuner.ai simplifies AI development, allowing users to focus on their unique use cases and ideas.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">4.1. Access the API tab for an overview of the required tokens and parameters to connect your chatbot to your app using REST API endpoints.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The Fine-Tuner REST API provides API endpoints for Fine-Tuner data types that allow to interact with your AI models remotely by sending and receiving JSON</li>
<li>Authentication to the Fine-Tuner API is performed via HTTP Bearer Authentication</li>
<li>Front end: Bubble</li>
</ul>

<li>GitWit uses a GPT-based agent to generate code and git to track changes made to files</li>
<li>GitWit ties together large language models and modern developer tools</li>
<li>It can spawn and modify codebases using just a single prompt</li>
<li>GitWit is primarily aimed at full-stack developers, and is particularly loved by those with a learning mindsetâ€”such as those learning a new stack or technology</li>
<li>It is in early beta and may require some experimentation with the prompts you enter</li>
<li>You are offered to choose from code bases:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>React + NextJS</li>
<li>Python using pip</li>
<li>A Chrome extension written in JavaScript</li>
<li>An AngularJS using npm.</li>
<li>Custom stack</li>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Enables users to create and instruct modular AI agents, generate document indexes for question-answering, and attach tools to agents for enhanced functionalities.</li>
<li>Facilitates coding assistance and conversational capabilities through predefined agents, along with the option to design custom agents, all within a keyboard and mouse-friendly terminal interface.</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-141" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-141"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Kompas AI is an advanced AI assistant for your team.</li>
<li>It's designed to assist and enhance your productivity.</li>
<li>It processes multiple tasks simultaneously.</li>
<li>Kompas AI outperforms ChatGPT Pro in response speed, using Microsoft Azure's OpenAI Service.</li>
<li>Kompas AI offers a free trial that allows you to use the Pro version for 10 days.</li>
<li>Kompas AI primarily uses the gpt-4-turbo, gpt-4-vision and gpt-3.5-turbo models, but it also supports other models like Gemini, Claude 2, and open-source models. Notably, Kompas AI features a larger context window, through gpt-4-turbo utilizing a 128K tokens Context Window that allows it to remember up to 512,000 characters of past conversation for more complex tasks.</li>
<li>Kompas AI prioritizes data security. Your files are protected with strong encryption, and data in transit is safeguarded. Unused data is regularly removed from the system.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-144" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-144"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A platform for creating your personal AI workflows and apps. Lutra first converses with you to understand your goals, and then writes code to produce AI workflows.</li>
<li>These AI workflows are akin to specialized agents that help you with all kinds of tasks. Because these workflows are based in code, Lutra is able to securely and reliably execute them, ensuring that your data is always protected.</li>
<li>Get a personalized newsletter everyday with concise summaries of news tailored to your interests.</li>
<li>Have AI automatically label your incoming emails into categories you choose. Get things done!</li>
<li>Collect public information about a person and the company they work for, so that you can be ready when you meet them.</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Makedraft is an AI that generates frontend code based on your instructions. You can then copy the HTML to any project</li>

<li>Makedraft will be introducing a Showcase for people to see Showcase projects. Makedraft is currently in open beta and is free to use. A Pro plan will be available soon. Users who subscribe to the Pro plan will have have their generated projects set to private by default</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">é€šè¿‡ MultiOn é¢„è®¢èˆªç­æˆ–è®¢è´­æ±‰å ¡</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/97adbdb6cb1fc731caf84ad4fc0a50eec3c9b5b82c76b1c1dd4f5198d5ef0fd5/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f70726f66696c655f696d616765732f313733353639393634373734343836343235362f6a724b4a574d37385f343030783430302e6a7067"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/97adbdb6cb1fc731caf84ad4fc0a50eec3c9b5b82c76b1c1dd4f5198d5ef0fd5/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f70726f66696c655f696d616765732f313733353639393634373734343836343235362f6a724b4a574d37385f343030783430302e6a7067" alt="image" data-canonical-src="https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_images/1735699647744864256/jrKJWM78_400x400.jpg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-148" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-148"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Productivity, General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-147" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-147"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The agent runs and controls the local Google Chrome, which allows it to interact with the world/services/web apps, just like people interact with the world/services/web apps using Google Chrome</li>
<li>The agent itself probably also runs locally and currently, it needs the local Google Chrome to function</li>
<li>Our understanding from the demo video is that they use local code and a custom plugin in ChatGPT to control a web browser (e.g., Google Chrome). This setup enables MultiOn to perform tasks like ordering plane tickets as if a human were interacting with the browser directly</li>
<li>Use cases
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A lot of cool real use cases, e.g.,
-Sending an email fully autonomously
-Posting a tweet
-Sending a tweet reply to a specific person with a specific message
-Sending a Facebook message to a friend
-Searching for vacation rentals and check pricing for an upcoming trip
-Searching for a wedding venue and starting the wedding planning process
-Scheduling a car wash</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>After introducing the GPT function calling, MultiOn can call itself recursively to spawn more sub-agents</li>
<li>Instead of calling multiple functions or APIs you just need one Universal Function that can interact with all services and have it call itself to accomplish more complex tasks in parallel</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Questflow is a marketplace designed for SMBs to connect with autonomous AI workers.</li>
<li>Our platform enables digital workers to discover and deploy AI agents for seamless workflow automation.</li>
<li>With a no-code editor, we empower digital knowledge providers to create, distribute, and monetize AI workers.</li>
<li>Similar to Upwork, Questflow offers a marketplace where users can utilize AI agents to accomplish tasks across various digital workspaces.</li>
<li>Creators have the opportunity to transform their specialized knowledge into AI agents, expanding their reach and generating revenue.</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto">v0 is a generative user interface system by Vercel Labs powered by AI. It generates copy-and-paste friendly React code based on Shadcn UI and Tailwind CSS.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Currently in waitlist stage</li>
<li>v0 generates custom components on the fly that you can copy and paste into your existing codebase</li>
<li>Built on NextJS App Router</li>
<li>AI by the Vercel <code>ai</code> SDK</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">âœ´ï¸</font></font><a href="https://www.superagent.sh/" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">è¶…çº§ä»£ç†</font></font></a></h3><a id="user-content-eight_pointed_black_star-superagent" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šï¼šeight_pointed_black_starï¼šè¶…çº§ç‰¹å·¥" href="#eight_pointed_black_star-superagent"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<details>
<p dir="auto">Superagent uses E2B as a <a href="https://x.com/pelaseyed/status/1709592941226831916?s=20" rel="nofollow">code execution tool</a>. To try Superagent with E2B, create a Code interpreter API and then select it for your agent to use.</p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">âœ´ï¸ </font></font><a href="https://e2b.dev/docs/llm-platforms/openai/" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">OpenAI çš„åŠ©æ‰‹</font></font></a></h3><a id="user-content-eight_pointed_black_star-openais-assistants" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼š:eight_pointed_black_starï¼šOpenAI çš„åŠ©æ‰‹" href="#eight_pointed_black_star-openais-assistants"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<details>
<p dir="auto">You can define actions for your AI assistant and E2B will automatically execute them inside a sandbox. This allows you to create powerful AI assistants with custom tools completely predefined by you.
To <a href="https://e2b.dev/docs/llm-platforms/openai" rel="nofollow">try the OpenAI Assistants with E2B</a>, you can follow our guide in <a href="https://e2b.dev/docs/llm-platforms/openai#python" rel="nofollow">Python</a> or <a href="https://e2b.dev/docs/llm-platforms/openai#java-script" rel="nofollow">JavaScript</a>.</p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">âœ´ï¸Langchain</font></font><a href="https://python.langchain.com/docs/integrations/tools/e2b_data_analysis" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">æ•°æ®åˆ†æå¸ˆ</font></font></a></h3><a id="user-content-eight_pointed_black_star-langchain-data-analyst" class="anchor" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼š:eight_pointed_black_starï¼šLangchain æ•°æ®åˆ†æå¸ˆ" href="#eight_pointed_black_star-langchain-data-analyst"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<details>
<p dir="auto">E2B Data Analysis sandbox <a href="https://python.langchain.com/docs/integrations/tools/e2b_data_analysis" rel="nofollow">integrated into Langchain</a> allows you to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Run Python code</li>
<li>Generate charts via matplotlib</li>
<li>Install Python packages dynamically during runtime</li>
<li>Install system packages dynamically during runtime</li>
<li>Run shell commands</li>
<li>Upload and download files.
See also a guide <a href="https://e2b.dev/blog/build-ai-data-analyst-with-langchain-and-e2b" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</li>
</ul>
</details>
